(**
In this file, we show how any linear category induces a linear/non-linear model.
This boils down to proving that the Eilenberg-Moore category of the (symmetric monoidal) comonad, given by a linear category, is cartesian monoidal.
*)


Notation "_ ≠ _" was already used in scope nat_scope.
[notation-overridden,parsing,default]

· # (linear_category_bang 𝕃) (f · (pr11 i · r)) =
f · pr11 i · pr21 bb
· # (linear_category_bang 𝕃) r
# (linear_category_bang 𝕃) (pr11 i · r) =
identity (linear_category_bang 𝕃 (pr11 aa))

  (linear_category_bang 𝕃)

  (linear_category_bang 𝕃) ⟦ aa, bb ⟧
f: 𝕃 ⟦ pr11 xx, pr11 aa ⟧
f_i_coalg: pr21 xx
· # (linear_category_bang 𝕃) (f · pr11 i) =
f · pr11 i · pr21 bb
r: 𝕃 ⟦ pr11 bb, pr11 aa ⟧
ir_id: is_retraction (pr11 i) r
p: pr21 xx
· # (linear_category_bang 𝕃) (f · (pr11 i · r)) =
f · pr11 i · pr21 bb
· # (linear_category_bang 𝕃) r
# (linear_category_bang 𝕃) (pr11 i · r) =
# (linear_category_bang 𝕃) (identity (pr11 aa))

      exact ir_id.
  Qed.

  𝕃 x: commutative_comonoid 𝕃

                 ((pr11 (linear_category_bang 𝕃)) x)))
         :
         pr21 xx
         · # (pr11 (linear_category_bang 𝕃))
             (hx · linear_category_comult 𝕃 x) =
         hx · linear_category_comult 𝕃 x
         · dialgebra_disp_tensor_op
             (identity_fmonoidal (pr1 𝕃))
             (lax_monoidal_from_symmetric_monoidal_comonad
                (pr2 𝕃) (linear_category_bang 𝕃))

                ((pr11 (linear_category_bang 𝕃)) x)

             (identity
                ((pr11 (linear_category_bang 𝕃)) x)
              · δ (linear_category_bang 𝕃) x))
        :
        (λ f : pr1 𝕃 ⟦ pr11 xx,
               pr11 ((eilenberg_moore_cofree 𝕃 x : EM)
                     ⊗ (eilenberg_moore_cofree 𝕃 x
                        :
                        EM)) ⟧,
         pr21 xx -->[
         f] pr21 ((eilenberg_moore_cofree 𝕃 x : EM)
                  ⊗ (eilenberg_moore_cofree 𝕃 x : EM)))
          (hx · linear_category_comult 𝕃 x))),, tt)
 apply transport_comonoid_from_free_lem.
  Qed.

f: sym_monoidal_cat_co_eilenberg_moore
  (linear_category_bang 𝕃) ⟦ x, y ⟧
transported_comonoid_counit_data
  (linear_category_cocommutative_comonoid 𝕃 (pr11 x))
  (pr21 x) =
pr21 x · # (pr11 (linear_category_bang 𝕃)) (pr11 f)
· linear_category_counit 𝕃 (pr11 y)
